DECLARE @var sysname;
SELECT @var = [d].[name]
FROM [sys].[default_constraints] [d]
INNER JOIN [sys].[columns] [c] ON [d].[parent_column_id] = [c].[column_id] AND [d].[parent_object_id] = [c].[object_id]
WHERE ([d].[parent_object_id] = OBJECT_ID(N'[Purchases]') AND [c].[name] = N'CustomerId');
IF @var IS NOT NULL EXEC(N'ALTER TABLE [Purchases] DROP CONSTRAINT [' + @var + '];');
UPDATE [Purchases] SET [CustomerId] = 0 WHERE [CustomerId] IS NULL;
ALTER TABLE [Purchases] ALTER COLUMN [CustomerId] int NOT NULL;
ALTER TABLE [Purchases] ADD DEFAULT 0 FOR [CustomerId];
CREATE INDEX [IX_Purchases_CustomerId] ON [Purchases] ([CustomerId]);
